TITLE       Measurement of Transuranium Isotopes Fission Cross    41369  1    3 
            Section with Lead Neutron Slowing-Down Spectrometer   41369  1    4 
AUTHOR     (V.F.Gerasimov, V.V.Danichev, V.N.Dement'ev,           41369  1    5 
            V.S.Zenkevich, G.V.Mozolev)                           41369  1    6 
INSTITUTE  (4RUSKUR)                                              41369  1    7 
REFERENCE  ((S,ISINN-5,348,199705)=(S,JINR-E3-97-213,348,199705)) 41369  1    8 
            Main Ref. Table of group c-s. Figs. of point-wise c-s.41369  1    9 
           ((S,ISINN-5,361,199705)=(S,JINR-E3-97-213,361,199705)) 41369  1   10 
                Details of spectrometer. Graphs of point-wise c-s.41369  1   11 
REL-REF    (M,40993001,V.F.Gerasimov+,C,87KIEV,3,84,1987)         41369  1   12 
            Details of method.                                    41369  1   13 
FACILITY   (LINAC,4RUSKUR)  Linear Accelerator 'Fakel'            41369  1   14 
                  combined   with lead slowing-down spectrometer. 41369  1   15 
INC-SOURCE (PHOTO) Electron beam energy 50 MeV, repetition rate   41369  1   16 
            275 Hz, current in pulse up to 1 A .                  41369  1   17 
           Carbon plate 1mm thick served as electron beam monitor.41369  1   18 
           Neutron flow was measured by Li-6(n,a)H-3 reaction.    41369  1   19 
           FAKEL generate up to 10**12 neutrons in the pulse.     41369  1   20 
SAMPLE      Samples were prepared in Radium Inst. (4RUSRI) by     41369  1   21 
            one technique on same backings.                       41369  1   22 
METHOD     (SLODT)  Slowing-down time in lead.                    41369  1   23 
           Spectrometer resolution function parameterized using   41369  1   24 
            the 39.93 eV resonance of 237Np(n,f) by Pearson       41369  1   25 
           distribution :                                         41369  1   26 
             n(z)=[1+(z-a0)**2/w**2]**(-a)*exp[u*atan[(z-a0)/w]]  41369  1   27 
            with                                                  41369  1   28 
             a=1.65, a0=0.978, w=0.101, u=0.82.                   41369  1   29 
             Pearson distribution was used in analysis to restore 41369  1   30 
             cross-sections in resonance region.                  41369  1   31 
            A gaussian approximation of the resolution function is41369  1   32 
             (dE/E)FWHM=a**2+b/E+cE)**(1/2)                       41369  1   33 
            with                                                  41369  1   34 
             a=0.32,  b=0.155 eV, c=2.52*10**(-5) eV**(-1).       41369  1   35 
            (Gaussian parameters were defined by V.Shorin,        41369  1   36 
            absent in publication. Gaussian approximation was used41369  1   37 
            for comparison of experimental and evaluated data.)   41369  1   38 
DETECTOR   (FISCH,PPAC) Fission chamber with 8 avalanche          41369  1   39 
           plane-parallel counters. Filled with heptane to        41369  1   40 
           pressure 20 Torr.                                      41369  1   41 
            The ratio of the same type detectors efficiency and   41369  1   42 
           their constancy were determined and checked during the 41369  1   43 
           experiments from Cf-252 spontaneous fission.           41369  1   44 
ANALYSIS   Time spectra of each detector were divided channel-    41369  1   45 
            wise into the time spectrum of 235U(n,f).             41369  1   46 
           The later was transformed into energetic ones using    41369  1   47 
            the normalized fission cross section of 235U(n,f).    41369  1   48 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-1,,3.) Error of nuclei quantities ratio for the   41369  1   49 
           analyzed samples and the standard sample of U-235.     41369  1   50 
           (ERR-2,,2.) Error of counter efficiencies ratio.       41369  1   51 
           (ERR-3,,3.) Error of U-235 reference cross section     41369  1   52 
           normalization.                                         41369  1   53 
           (ERR-4,,3.) Error of experimental data correction      41369  1   54 
            procedure.                                            41369  1   55 
           Channelwise statistical error of the original exp. data41369  1   56 
           is smoothed over and its contribution is negligible in 41369  1   57 
           the majority of group cross section.                   41369  1   58
